 saal 1913 main 29 november ko uttar pradesh ke gonda zile ke balrampur main unka janm hua tha
 He studied up to high school there and went to Aligarh Muslim University for further studies
 yahaan unhen us samay ke mashhoor or ubharate hue shaayaron kii sangat mili

 yah vah daur tha jab desh gulam tha or angrezon ke khilaaf aazaadee andolan kii neenv kaaphi pehle pad chuki thi
 The freedom movement's passion was on the youth
 ali sardaar jaafaree bhi unheen main shumaar the
 The result was that during one such movement, Sardar was evicted from the university in a crime of strike against members of the Executive Council of the voiceroy
 par sardaar to sardaar the
 He passed his BA from anglo-arabic College Delhi and earned an MA degree from Lucknow University
 is dauraan chaatr-andolanon main bhaag lene kaa unka jazbaa kam nahin hua
 Ali Sardar Jafri traveled to the freedom movement and even after that, where he met Khurrat colleagues of the Progressive Writers Association, including Sajjad Zaheer
 unheen ke prabhaav main sardaar ne vladimir iliich ulyanov lenin va karl henrikh marks ko padhaa
 It was from here that his thinking and guidance got the solid ground of Marxism, Communism
 apni samyavaadee vichaardhaara ke chalate vah pragatisheel lekhak sangh se jud gaye
 During this time, he not only read the ideas of foreign thinkers like Pablo Neruda and Luiranga, including Indian litterateurs like Premchand, Rabindranath Thakur, Faiz Ahmed 'faiz', Mulk Raj Anand, but also adopted what he learned, knowing his ideas, literature
 us daur ke kaabil or behtareen aalimon kii sangat kaa asar yah hua ki ali sardaar jaafaree ek aise shaayar ke rup main ubharen jinaki shaayari mehanatakashon ke dukh-dard kaa aainaa thi
 Jaffrey's literary journey began in 1938 with the publication of a short story collection called 'manzil'
 par isse pehle hi 1936 main vah lakhanu main progressive riters movement ke pehle sammelan kii adhyakshata kar chuke the
 In 1939 he became the co-editor of the literary journal 'nayaadab' of the Progressive Writers' Movement, which was published until 1949
 unhone gyaarah kavy-sangrah, chaar gadhy sangrah, do kahani sangrah or ek naatak ke alaava khub saare padya evam gadhy likhe or apane daur kii saahitiyik patr patrikaon main likhte rahe
 His first collection of poetry 'parvaz' appeared in 1944
 vah kai saamaajik, siyaasi or saahitiyik andolanon main lagaataar shaamil rahe

 This organization was then banned

 unki khyaati ek aise shaayar ke rup main rahi he, jisane urdu shaayari main chand-mukt kavita kii parampara shuru kii
 He was close to Hindavi despite being in Urdu
 unki shaayari kii bhashaa itani saral he ki uske arth apane bhav ke saath jhalkate hai

 unki shaayari ke kuch udaahranon ko dekhen to, 'jab nahin aae the tum, tab bhi to tum aae the', 'gaay ke than se nikalati he chamakati chaandi', 'dhuen se kaale tave bhi chingaarion ke hotho se hans rahe hai', 'imaliyon ke patton par dhoop par sukhaati he', 'meri vaadi main wo ek din yun hi aa nikali thi', 'abhi or tej kar le sar-e-khanjar-e-adaa ko', 'tum se berangi-e-hasti kaa gilaa karnaa tha', 'mere darvaaze se ab chaand ko rukhsat kar do' aadi urdu shaayari main nae lahaze kii pahchaan ko bataane ke liye kaaphi hai
 Ali Sardar Jafri also contributed to Indian cinema
 ek geetkaarake rup main unke mahatvapurn kaamon main 'jaljla', 'dharti ke laal' or 'paradesi' jaisi filmon kaa geet lekhan shaamil he
 Between the years 1948 to 1978, he wrote 'nayi Duniya Ko Salaam', 'khoon ki streak', 'aman ka star', 'asia awakened', 'stone wall', 'ek khwab', 'parhan-e-nafi' And wrote collections like 'lahu Pukarta Hai', which enriched Indian literature
 iske alaava unhone 'meraa safar' jaisi prasiddh rachana bhi likhi

 is sangrah kii ek pankti un dinon khub mashhoor hui, ‘guftugu band na ho, baat se baat chale, subh tak shaam-e-mulaaqaat chale, ham pe hansati hui ye taron bhari raat chale’’

 unhone ipta ke liye do naatak bhi likhe

 Indian Railways is currently testing South Africa's ultrasonic broken rail detection system to automatically test thousands of thousands of kilometers of rail tracks spread across the country
 kai jagah chal rahaa tryultrasonic broken rail ditection system dakshin africa ke raksha vibhaag dwaara taiyaar kii gai vah takanic he jisamen ultrasonic tarangon kaa istemaal karke rail patariyon ke fracture ko samay rahete janaa ja saktaa he

 This is how ultrasonic brokered rail detection system uses the guided wave of ultrasonic waves, in this technique the track of the rail track is checked every minute using ultrasound waves around the joints in a 1 km long rail track
 If there is a possibility of wear and tear in the track, then the alarm of the system goes to the concerned railway department

 Ultrasonic waves are analyzed by an automatic computer system, as soon as any interference is noticed, this information automatically goes into the system, after which the system issues an alarm

 tippaniyan Official sources said, it will be the largest event in the world
 smart india haikathan 36 ghante tak bina ruke chalane vaali digital programing pratiyogita he jisamen chaatro kii timen saamne rakhi gayi kisi bhi samasya ke abhinav hal talashne ke liye ek duusare se pratispardhaa karengi

 Reliance Jio has started its services from 5 September

 tri ne paaya he ki ye oparator license sharton kaa anupaalan nahin kar rahe hai
 TRAI said, 'the secret motive for not providing interconnection is to hinder competition and it is anti-consumer'

 imran hasni ne kaha, ‘‘nirdeshak nikhil adwani ne is film main jabardast prayog kiya he
